00021  *
00022  *
00023  * Overview:    contains numerical constants for theories of Nutation,
00024  *              tidal variations in UT and Polar motion, etc..
00025  *              see SbGeoRefFrame.H for classes' interface.
00026  *              Implemented (i.e., typed):
00027  *              * the IAU 1980 theory of nutation;
00028  *              * the IAU 1996 theory of nutation;
00029  *              * daily and sub-daily tidal variations in EOP from Ray, 1995;
00030  *              * daily and sub-daily tidal variations in EOP JPL-92 Model (Sovers et al., 1993);
00031  *              * daily and sub-daily tidal variations in EOP Herring-Dong Model, 1994;
00032  *
00033  */
00034
